 You must have heard these chaupaiyas of Hanuman Chalisa but do you know their true meaning? What is the importance of siddhis and funds? Shri Ram Bhakta Hanuman was given the boon of eight siddhis and nine funds by mother Janaki and says that the power to handle them also Mahabali was only in Hanuman
 - duniya main sabase keemtee vasteen hai- nau nidhiyaan jinhen paa lene ke baad kisi bhi prakaar ke dhan or sampatti kii aavashyaktaa nahin rahati hai
 Likewise, Ashta Siddhi is the greatest power in the world, after attaining a person becomes all-powerful - these funds and accomplishments cannot be found in normal condition - special grace of God is necessary to get these- Funds and accomplishments It is not a big thing to be found, it is very difficult to keep them with you - if there is a slight mistake, these funds and achievements can also be snatched away - only Numan ji is the only God who is blessed with eight siddhis and nine funds - and by worshiping Hanuman ji, these siddhis and funds can also be attained only by the grace of Hanuman ji, a person can get these eight siddhis and nine funds
 But surprisingly it is that those who do devotion to Mahabali Hanuman do not want any accomplishment, nor wish for funds
 jaankaron kii maane to agar kisi vyakti ko ye siddhiyaan yaa nidhiyaan praapt ho jaaen to wo sansar kii koi bhi cheez hasil kar saktaa he
 Glory of Siddhis and Funds? - In total, there are eight types - Anima, Laghima, Dignity, Attainment, Prakamya, Mahima, Ishita and subdivision - The things which are very rare are called funds, they are mentioned in the cosmic Purana and Vayu Purana
 Nine of these are the major funds

 ) In the light of Indian constitution and laws, the Central Government has not been able to provide the information sought under the Right to Information (RTI) about the meaning and definition of the word 'hindu'
 madhya pradesh ke neemuch nivasee saamaajik kaaryakarta chandrashekhar gaur ne ravivaar ko bataaya ki unhone artiai ke tahat arji daayar kar poocha tha ki bhartiya samvidhan or kanoonon ke anusaar 'hindu' shabd kaa aashay or paribhaasha kya he
 He said, 'on my RTI application sent by the Ministry of Home Affairs, Government of India on 31 July, it was stated that the requisite information is not available with the Central Public Information Officer (CPIO)
 ' gaur ne apane artiai aavedan main sarkaar se yah bhi jaananaa chaha tha ki desh main kin aadhaaron par kisi samudaay ko hindu mana jaataa he or hinduon ko bahusnkhyakon kii tarah dekha jaataa he

 ' The social worker said, 'the government's response to my RTI application is shocking
 agar sarkaar ko yah pataa hi nahin he ki hindu shabd kaa aashay or paribhaasha kya he, to hindu vivaah adhinium sareekhe kanoon aakhir kis aadhaar par bana die gaye
 'gaur said,' The government should also explain why it asks citizens to identify their religious identity while filling different government forms and why the population figures are released on religious grounds
 ' tippaniyan Famous thinker KN Govindacharya, when asked about the government's reply to the RTI application filed on the word 'hindu', said, 'the concept of government in Hindustan came out through the Indian Government Act of 1935, while the subject of Hindutva is thousands of years old

 This society is run by the state, along with the religion, society and minority
 rajasatta ko is baat se waakif hone kii jarurat he

 cook ne 40 gendon main paanch chauke kii madad se 22 ran banaae

 shami ahamed kii gend par rabindra jadeja ne unka kaich lapka

 a 79-run partnership between Ian Bell and Root for the third wicket
 isse pehle, bhartiya team ne suresh raina (83) kii shandaar ardhshtkeey pari kii badaulat toss haarane ke baad kharaab shuruyaat se ubarte hue 49
 Losing all wickets in 4 overs, scored 226 runs
 ek samay bharat ne 78 ranon par paanch wicket ganvaa die the, lekin raina ne rabindra jadeja (39) ke saath milakar score ko sammanjanak sthiti main pahunchaaya
 Raina hit eight fours and two sixes in his fine knock of 98 balls, while Jadeja hit one four and two sixes in 65 balls
 donon ne chathe wicket ke liye 78 ranon kii saajhedaari nibhaai
 Among the lower order batsmen, Ravichandran Ashwin contributed 19 runs while Bhuvneshwar Kumar contributed 31 runs
 kumaar or aswin ne aathven wicket ke liye bahumoolya 34 ran jode
 Kumar 225 and Shami Ahmed (1) were out for a total of 226 runs
 kumaar ne apni 30 gendon kii pari main paanch chauke lagaae
 Apart from this, Gautam Gambhir contributed 24 runs for India
 england kii ore se tim bresnan ne chaar wicket liye
 Apart from this, Stuart Finn, Tim Bresnan and James Treadwell took two wickets each
 bharat kii shuruyaat acchhee nahin rahi
 Rohit Sharma, who hit a brilliant half-century in Mohali, was caught by James Bredwell in the second slip off Tim Bresnan for a four-run total, while Virat Kohli did not allow Bresnan to open the account
 inkaa kaich bhi tradewell ne lapka
 Rohit's wicket fell to a total of 13 runs, while Kohli was also out on the same total
 iske baad yuvaraj singh 24 ran ke kul yoga par chalate bane
 His wicket was taken by Stuart Finn
 gambheer kaa wicket 49 ranon ke kul yoga par gira
 Yuvraj could not even open the account, while Gambhir scored 24 runs off 42 balls with the help of five fours
 gambheer ko tradewell ne apni gend par ian bel ke haathon kaich karaayaa
 After this, captain Mahendra Singh Dhoni (14) and Raina shared a 30-run partnership for the fifth wicket
 dhoni ne 23 gendon par do chauke lagaae
 His wicket fell at a total of 79 runs
 bharat ne mohali main khele gaye chauthe mukaable main paanch wicket kii jeet ke saath yah shrunkhlaa 3-1 se apane naam kar lee thi
 The first match was played in Rajkot, which was won by the English team
 iske baad bharat ne kochi, ranchi or mohali main hetric lagaakar elister cook ko post kiya tha
 It was a historic moment for the HPCA Stadium, located at an altitude of 1500 meters above sea level, for the first time an international match was played on this picturesque ground
 isse pehle yah indian premier lig maichon kii mejabani kar chukaa he, lekin antarrashtriya patal par aane kaa ise pehali baar mauka mila he
 The comments buddha dharmaguru dalai lamas ke nivas sthal ke taur par duniyabar main mashhoor is shandaar paryaton sthal ko pehle hi vishwa maanchitr par jagah mili hui he
 But today it is included in the record book as a new international cricket venue
